<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1c67d8a5-9b36-42e2-b33e-77507a98d7f6'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText6262962494746174462" style="display:none">How do you keep existing when your heart is so splintered, so completely torn to shreds, your pulse is fading?<br /><br />You’re… broken. How do you move forward when every breath is nothing more than a constant ache? Living becomes an insidious reminder that you threw away the single largest part of yourself. Your… soul. No amount of distraction can pull you from the torture of losing your… life.<br /><br />Now that Emily Cooper has walked away from her first love, she finds herself running toward her only love. Unraveling fast, but clinging to hope, Emily risks all she has left on the man that has consumed her every thought and dream since the day they met. Will Gavin take her back? And if so, will their reunion be a collision of two hearts destined to complete one another and rekindle a love that knew no boundaries? Or will scars from their past rip open, tearing slowly at what each of them was meant to be? Can fate, the ultimate game changer, mend the shattered road it laid out from the start?<br /><br />Only time will tell…<br /><br />Tick-Tock…</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer640669797" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7069239433807787868"><a href='http://www.angiesdreamyreads.com/2013/07/blog-tour-pulse-by-gail-mchugh-review.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>This Review was Posted at Angie's Dreamy Reads!</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“A romance that is food for the soul and a love story that is simply unforgettable.” - Angie's Dreamy Reads</i>
</b><br/><br/>Have you ever read a book or series that has seeped so heavily into your veins, your body, your mind that you think of nothing else? A book that has filled every void, every fiber within your heart and soul. A book you could read again and again and again. There are some books that you could never get sick of. Some that the characters come </span>
  <span id="freeText7069239433807787868" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.angiesdreamyreads.com/2013/07/blog-tour-pulse-by-gail-mchugh-review.html" rel="nofollow noopener">This Review was Posted at Angie's Dreamy Reads!</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“A romance that is food for the soul and a love story that is simply unforgettable.” - Angie's Dreamy Reads</i>
</b><br><br>Have you ever read a book or series that has seeped so heavily into your veins, your body, your mind that you think of nothing else? A book that has filled every void, every fiber within your heart and soul. A book you could read again and again and again. There are some books that you could never get sick of. Some that the characters come alive and embed themselves into every pore of your being. Collide and Pulse is that series for me. It's a series that I breathe, think and dream about. To be Emily Cooper and to be loved by a man like Gavin Blake. To be loved in such a way that you are cherished, savored and consumed. To own another human being the way Gavin and Emily own each other. To live the experience she had. I want that. I need that. This book has created that in me. The need to live through every line, every word, every paragraph. The author writes so beautifully, so eloquently that every page is a beautiful experience and a journey that's simply unforgettable. I have a lot of favorite books. Books that I have absolutely loved but this series is my favorite. It's a series that I care deeply about. The characters have come alive in me and are my friends that I love and cherish. Pulse is an emotional journey. One that puts you through the ringer. One that will make you laugh, cry and swoon. It'll crush your heart, your spirit, give you intense heart palpitations and then put you back together. It's what I call a "book experience!" You’re not simply reading the story, you're living the story. Each and every part. It's a romance that's unforgettable. It's breathtaking and heart stopping. What I consider to be a <b>MUST, MANDATORY AND REQUIRED READ!</b> <br><br><br><b>
  <i>****** If you have NOT read Collide please stop here and go read it. This is not a spoiler review but there are things that will spoil Collide if you have not read it! ******</i>
</b><br><br><br>Ok, so when we last left Gavin and Emily they were apart. Emily had left Dillon and rejected Gavin. It was heartbreaking to watch Gavin get his heart broken by the woman he loves and made me sick that Emily hadn’t provided Gavin with the benefit of the doubt that he did nothing wrong. With Emily's departure after she leaves the "asshole" Dillon we are left broken. Broken for Em, broken for Gavin but there's a flicker of hope. Hope that they still have a chance. Emily knows she made the wrong choice. She feels it in every, bone, pour and fiber in her body. She needs to get her man back!! And that's exactly what she does. She goes to get Gavin but Gavin's not home. Gavin's MIA. <br><br>After getting his heart broken Gavin needs to get away. He needs to escape from everything that reminds him of Emily. She has single handedly fucked him up. She's messed with his heart, mind and body and he simply can't cope. He decides to get on an airplane and head for Mexico where he can drown his sorrows and try to recover. <br><br>When Emily hears that Gavin's gone she books a ticket to go fight for the man she should have never let go. Determined to apologize and get him back she goes to the hotel Gavin's staying at and what greets her is intense. Things between her and Gavin are rocky (obviously). Gavin's not sure he can trust Emily and be with her. She's unequivocally broken him down and he's afraid that she's going to up and leave him for Dillon. The back and forth is angsty but all is made right or so we think. Just when things are getting back on track an unexpected situation arises and Dillon is thrust into their lives again. Life gets rocky and Emily and Gavin relationship goes through the unthinkable. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>Can they move past all the new challenges with the baggage they hold from the past? <br><br>Can Emily give Gavin what he needs and heal her broken spirit at the same time? <br><br>Will Gavin be able to trust that Emily isn’t going to bolt when things get tough? <br><br>Can their love survive?</i>
</b> <br><br><br>Get ready for a ride that is going to have you hanging on. Gail McHugh can write and she can write fantastically. You’ll be in book hangover mode when this is all said and done. <br><br>With all that said I want to talk a little about Emily and Gavin. Sigh....This is hard for me to write because I loved these characters so much. Emily...I know she got a lot of slack at the end of the first book. She was frustrating and at times you wanted to shake her but even through all that I loved her. I wasn’t overly annoyed or frustrated. I understood. I understood the way she felt, the way she thought and the way she processed her situations. Emily was a broken woman. She was a shell of a person. That happened over time throughout her life as the events that took place shaped her; the loss of her mother, the abuse she saw from her father to her mother and the slow decaying abuse of her spirit from Dillon. These are life moments that <b>BREAK</b> people. That's why her decision making was so flawed and that's why I was able to look past it and see a woman with potential. A woman looking for love and not knowing where to find it. She found that in Gavin but was scared. Scared to risk her heart. She takes the leap in Pulse and you can literally see her bloom like a flower opening one petal at a time. She grows and blossoms. It's beautiful and makes me teary just thinking about it. I can say with all honesty that she is my most beloved female character. She starts out weak but finishes strong!! She loves and inspires. She is for me a woman after my own heart and in her I see glimpses of myself. <br><br>Gavin! Oh sweet, sexy, bottle cap loving Gavin. I say this often because I think it's true. To me, Gavin is the perfect mix between Christian Grey (Fifty Shades) and Kellan (Thoughtless). He's the mega millionaire with a heart of gold. Sweet, seductive, possessive, smart, shmexy (lol) and just all around brilliant. He's the perfect catch. The kind of guy any girl would dream about bringing home to mom and dad. Gavin has a tenderness to him that really speaks to me and I think to a lot of woman. He can be an ass at times but under all that is a loving, tenderhearted, giving man. A man that would sacrifice himself for the woman he loves. Not only is Gavin (in my opinion) a sweetheart but he is a suave, smooth talking, son of a gun..lol! The lines..oh my..the lines out of his mouth are swoon worthy. He knows exactly what to say to a woman to leave her weak kneed and melty inside. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>“We were written for one another, and I wouldn't change one line in our romance novel. The good, the bad, the in between. It's ours. We own it.” - Gavin Blake <br><br>“When I look at you, I feel like I’m looking at the other half of myself. You’ve filled the empty space in my soul, and because of that, you’re a Goddess to me. That’s the way I’m always going to treat you. For the rest of your life. I promise you that.” - Gavin Blake <br><br>“I’m going to break you, Emily Cooper. I’m going to break you down and slowly build you back up. Second by second, piece by piece, and memory by memory.” - Gavin Blake </i>
</b><br><br><br>See...he melts my inside like warm, silky milk chocolate. He's dreamy, absolutely dreamy. I love the way he loves and protects Emily. I love the way he defends her. The way he wants to posses her mind, body and soul. You can feel his intense adoration for Emily through his words and actions and there is <b>NOTHING,</b> absolutely <b>NOTHING</b> sexier than that. <br><br>Overall this story is.... gosh, this story is ineffable. It’s a true romance. One that has ups and downs. I loved it. I loved every second of reading it. It's one of those series you'll savor and come back to time and time again. I also think it will become a series that is ingrained in your mind and will affect your future reads. It’s one that will be with you always. I wouldn't just recommend this...I would say <b>HURRY, GO NOW, READ IT, SAVOR IT, ENJOY IT</b> and get ready for journey that’s indescribably good. My rating is <b>5 MILLION</b> stars.<br><br><b>To read more and see the EXCLUSIVE Gavin Blake interview and enter a giveaway for a KINDLE FIRE, $100 AMAZON GIFTCARD, $250 VISA GIFTCARD, 2 SIGNED SETS OF COLLIDE AND PULSE, head over to Angie's Dreamy Reads.<b><br><br><a href="http://www.angiesdreamyreads.com/2013/07/blog-tour-pulse-by-gail-mchugh-review.html" rel="nofollow noopener">GIVEAWAY AND INTERVIEW LINK</a><br><br><b><u>This Ladies is MY (yes...MY) Gavin Blake...</u></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401682i/779977._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="7069239433807787868" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer10302046449489204283">5 Stars+++++++<br/><br/>This story is about more then a hot character that makes you swoon. This is a story about a broken woman who had the courage to leave an abusive relationship. A woman who finally realizes she's worth more then what she's allowed herself to believe. A woman who decides to risk it all and go after the one thing she really wants. A woman who decides that she deserves to be loved.   <span id="freeText10302046449489204283" style="display:none">5 Stars+++++++<br /><br />This story is about more then a hot character that makes you swoon. This is a story about a broken woman who had the courage to leave an abusive relationship. A woman who finally realizes she's worth more then what she's allowed herself to believe. A woman who decides to risk it all and go after the one thing she really wants. A woman who decides that she deserves to be loved. This is a story about a man who no matter what is thrown at him doesn't give up on the woman he was made to love. A man who does everything in his power to protect, love, and comfort his woman. This is a story about strength, growth, trust, love and forgiveness. <br /><br />This is a story that should be read by any woman who has or hasn't found themselves in an abusive relationship. <br /><br /><b>"Did you know one in three women wind up in a mentally or physically abusive relationship?" "But the funny part is, it doesn't start off that way. It starts off wonderful, as close to everything you imagined something solid should be. Then Little by little, the relationship changes, and you wonder if you're going crazy."</b><br /><br />This story starts off where Collide left off of. We see Emily deal with the after math of her decisions once she finally gets the courage to leave Dillon. If you already didn't love Gavin then you will fall even further in love with him. He truly is perfect. It's an emotional story that will leave you breathless, will have you laughing and definitely will have you crying. This story is so honest, real and true.<br /><br />It's so well written, and so brilliantly told you will not be disappointed. Gail thank you for writing this series. You really have no idea how many lives you will touch with this story and how many woman might realize they too are worth it after reading it.<br /><br />I won't give you anything more because you honestly need to go into this blindly. I highly recommend that you pick up this book.</span>

  <span id="freeText1218801684487515767" style="display:none"><br><br>3.5 Gavin Lovin' Stars!!!<br><br>Firstly I would like to apologize to all my fellow GR friends who thought this book was a 5 star read; sadly for me, it just wasn't...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795633.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Since these two seem to LOVE countdown's...<br>Here's my countdown as to WHY...<br><br>One: Dramatics in the start of the book.<br>Yes Emily told Gavin she's marrying dickward Dillon and Gavin ran away to Mexico to heal his broken heart and threw his phone onto the runway. See the dramatics?<br><br>Two: Emily realizes she made the biggest mistake of her life; she faces her fears of flying and goes after him.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795634.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I was ready to take that plunge and never look back. Never. I was ready to risk everything for you, to push away the overwhelming fear I had because I knew you and I are worth it. We fell in love in a second. I was barely able to blink, and you had my entire world upside-down. I was scared you weren’t… real. I was scared no one could be as magnetic as you are to me. I want a do-over so when you think of this road, this is what you’ll remember. Me holding you… you staring into my eyes… and us kissing.”</b><br><br>Three: The undying love between these two.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795636.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes, WE ALL KNOW how much they loved each other, it was written on EVERYSINGLE page, we could.not.miss.it even if we tried.<br><br><b>
  <i>"I want to break the rules with you. Kiss you passionately every day. Make you smile when you’re about to cry. I want no regrets with us. I want us to laugh together until we can’t breathe and it hurts. No man will ever love you the way I’m going to love you, Emily. You’re it. My last. My forever"</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795637._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I’m saying this because it’s said breaths are stolen during a passionate kiss. That’s not true, Gavin, because I literally can’t breathe before your lips even touch mine. I try, but I’m unable to. I can’t think when you look at me. You strip my mind bare. You always have, and it’s beautiful and consuming. It’s magical and everything a girl is supposed to feel. It’s said you’re truly in love with someone if your skin tingles from their touch. Mine tingles when I hear your voice; I don’t need you to touch me. I can feel you when you’re not near me. I feel you in my dreams. I felt you when you were a thousand miles away."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795638.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Four: Things were TOO good that you could anticipate something bad was going to happen because there was TOO much book left!<br><br><b>"Stay crazy, dangerous, reckless, and intoxicating with me. Just do it waking up by my side every morning.”</b><br><br>Yes, I figured this was coming...<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Emily is pregnant and doesn't know who the father is!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Five: Gavin's acceptance of this BIG revelation and again professing it UNDYING and forever love for Emily!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795639._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I’m going to break you, Emily Cooper. I’m going to break you down and slowly build you back up. Second by second, piece by piece, and memory by memory, I’m going to make you realize you’re worth what I’m going to give to you. If I have to open a dictionary every day and make you stare at the word ‘worth,’ I’ll do it.”</i>
</b><br><br>Six: Dillion the dickward!!! What a douche bag of note!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795640._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seven: Random chapters which make no sense and are completely useless (if you read the book you know what I'm talking about)<br><br>Eight: The outcome at the end was expected and seriously Emily, you couldn't wait??<br><br><u>Reasons why it atleast got 3.5 stars:</u><br><br>One: Gavin (that's reason enough) <br><br><b>
  <i>"When I look at you, I feel like I’m looking at the other half of myself. You’ve filled the empty space in my soul, and because of that, you’re a Goddess to me. That’s the way I’m always going to treat you. For the rest of your life. I promise you that. I fucking promise.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795641._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Two: The sex was Hot<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795642.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Three: Olivia! Love this bitch!!!! She's awesome!<br><br>Four: Gavin (have I mentioned this ;) )<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795643.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Its kind of sad that this wasn't better for me, again its the high expectations of sequels! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407395i/795644.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ok I'm bursting with love.. (Insert sarcasm)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407395ra/795645.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer513451257" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10250888810824327777"><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/McHughPulse2TitlebySueBee_zps8b67a3b4.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406209i/792221.jpg' alt=' photo McHughPulse2TitlebySueBee_zps8b67a3b4.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>★★★★! Pulse (book 2). The conclusion of Emily’s story. Down to one man, but still a roller-coaster of misunderstandings, jealousy, betrayal, lust & an intense against-all-odds love!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Do you know how scary it is to want something so bad you’re willing to change your whole life for it?”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><u>The triangle in Collide, book 1 has come to an end and a hero has emerged. I recommend you read this series as a set and in order:</u><br/>BOOK 1 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/491099310' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <b>Collide</b>
</a> <br/>BOOK 2 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/513451257' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <b>Pulse</b>
</a><br/><br/><i><b>Collide (book 1) follow</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText10250888810824327777" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/McHughPulse2TitlebySueBee_zps8b67a3b4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406209i/792221.jpg" alt=" photo McHughPulse2TitlebySueBee_zps8b67a3b4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★! Pulse (book 2). The conclusion of Emily’s story. Down to one man, but still a roller-coaster of misunderstandings, jealousy, betrayal, lust &amp; an intense against-all-odds love!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Do you know how scary it is to want something so bad you’re willing to change your whole life for it?”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><u>The triangle in Collide, book 1 has come to an end and a hero has emerged. I recommend you read this series as a set and in order:</u><br>BOOK 1 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/491099310" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Collide</b>
</a> <br>BOOK 2 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/513451257" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Pulse</b>
</a><br><br><i><b>Collide (book 1) followed Emily Cooper, who had just moved to New York to be closer to her stockbroker boyfriend Dillon Parker</b>. While working as a waitress she <b>encountered handsome mogul and playboy Gavin Blake</b> and sparks flew. But Emily resisted Gavin’s attempts at flirtation only to shortly thereafter realize that Gavin is her boyfriend’s close friend and VIP client. We then followed them in a love triangle while both men vied for Emily’s heart and Gavin came out the victor.</i><br><br><b>Pulse (book 2) opens up right after the cliffhanger ending of book 1</b>. Emily has made her decision she wants Gavin and now she only has to convince him she means it. <b>Follow Gavin and Emily on a journey as they learn to trust each other again while building a relationship only to have it tested over and over again</b>. <br><br>Gavin and Emily’s story is a <b>rollercoaster filled with intrigue, misunderstandings, deceit, betrayals, jealousy, lust and love </b>. Not surprisingly Dillon will play a part throughout this story as well. And just like in book 1 the story will keep you at the edge of your seat. <b>Thankfully most issues are resolved quickly, but some shadow their story until the very end</b>. I will say no more, their story is best experienced. <br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/McHughCollide1-2HerobySueBee_zps7c5af5ad.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402892i/783486.jpg" alt=" photo McHughCollide1-2HerobySueBee_zps7c5af5ad.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Gavin Blake</b> is the perfect hero. We learned in book 1 that there is much more to his façade of the jaded, bored, ultra-rich playboy. He is sweet, caring, kind and oh so very patient. Six words to describe <b>Gavin: Memorable, noble, intense, charming, captivating and… shmexy.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Third”— he grinned and leaned into her ear—” never in a billion years have couples fucked the way we do. We break records.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/McHughCollide1-2HeroinebySueBee_zps8fbad919.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402892i/783487.jpg" alt=" photo McHughCollide1-2HeroinebySueBee_zps8fbad919.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Emily Cooper</b> is what the story needed to keep the drama going and though she annoyed me at times I kept reminding myself, she is what Gavin wants. Five words to describe <b>Kate: Naïve, annoying, meek, endearing and kind.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Caveman much?”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>The Collide series took me on a bumpy ride</b>. But no matter how much Emily managed to annoyed me <b>I was very much rooting for them and their HEA</b>. While the writing was a bit long-winded and predictable at times I found it an enjoyable story! <br><br><b>Captivating plot! Perfect ending! Hot, shmexy and memorable hero! Overall an excellent read! Thanks Ms. McHugh!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Little did she know then, a stolen moment, a sweatshirt, many bottle caps, and few layers peeled back later, her life would never be the same.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5 stars <br>Heroine rating: 3 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 4.5 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 4 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 4 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 4 stars<br>Story ending rating: 4.5<br>Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 4 stars<br>************************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 4 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this series: Maybe later.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/tumblr_lkn6xat6zL1qzg930o1_500_zpsde5292d7.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_626764871" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/626764871" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/626764871?book_show_action=true">May 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17267122-pulse">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=cry-baby-books">cry-baby-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer626764871" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9108001596150534282"><b>It's LIVE! <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.com/Pulse-Collide-ebook/dp/B00DULA3B2/ref=wl_it_dp_o_pC_nS_nC?ie=UTF8&colid=2RK3REKZGD6WO&coliid=I4PXWMPVYMCZT'>http://www.amazon.com/Pulse-Collide-e...</a></b><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Our past is imperfect,<br/> <br/>but our future’s breathtaking.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423241i/843142._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='460' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Where to begin? I've been sitting on the knowledge of what was contained inside <b>Pulse</b> for a while now and it has been complete TORTURE not sharing it with the world. <br/><br/>I’ll start at the beginning….I read <i>Collide</i> and was irate with Emily Cooper's actions at the end of the book. I mean really? What the hell? Emily was on my most hated idiot female heroine list right under Keira from Thought</span>
  <span id="freeText9108001596150534282" style="display:none"><b>It's LIVE! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Pulse-Collide-ebook/dp/B00DULA3B2/ref=wl_it_dp_o_pC_nS_nC?ie=UTF8&amp;colid=2RK3REKZGD6WO&amp;coliid=I4PXWMPVYMCZT">http://www.amazon.com/Pulse-Collide-e...</a></b><br><br><br><b>
  <i>"Our past is imperfect,<br> <br>but our future’s breathtaking.”</i>
</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423241i/843142._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="460" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Where to begin? I've been sitting on the knowledge of what was contained inside <b>Pulse</b> for a while now and it has been complete TORTURE not sharing it with the world. <br><br>I’ll start at the beginning….I read <i>Collide</i> and was irate with Emily Cooper's actions at the end of the book. I mean really? What the hell? Emily was on my most hated idiot female heroine list right under Keira from Thoughtless. I can now shout it from the roof tops that with 100% certainty Gail McHugh completely redeemed Emily and that this read was absolutely <b>FANTASTIC</b>!! Authors should take notes from Gail because this is how you write a sequel!!!!! <br><br>This book is so well done and well written that there is NOTHING I would change. Gail McHugh is one hell of an author and this book is a full <b>5 stars</b> or more because the story deserves it. The characters evolved and grew although you may suffer heart palpitations, I wouldn’t have had it any other way. <br><br><i>Pulse</i> starts off right where <i>Collide</i> left off. Emily walks out of Dillon’s apartment and decides follow her heart…Gavin. Sadly, Emily’s day late and dollar short. After spilling his feelings all over the engagement party Gavin heads out of town and off the grid to lick his wounds figuring that the wedding is still on. Right from the get go…Emily isn’t overly crying or indecisive she goes for what she wants and puts her heart on the line. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Please forgive me for fighting against us in the beginning, Gavin. Please forgive me for not fighting for us when I knew we were supposed to be together.”</i>
</b><br><br>I’m not going to spoil any part of this story so let’s say Emily doesn’t disappoint she becomes the heroine a reader can relate to and love. <br><br>Gavin was swoon worthy, heart breaking and completely kick ass. He has a realness that is so endearing that I think he must be somewhere in Manhattan and this reader just has to keep up the search for him. <br><br><b>
  <i>”I’m going to break you Emily Cooper. I’m going to break you down, and slowly build you back up. Second by second, piece by piece, and memory by memory, I’m going to make you realize you’re worth what I’m going to give you.”</i>
</b><br><br>Dillon is Dillon and all the supporting characters were well done as well. Go forth and click purchase because this is one sequel that doesn’t fall short but surpasses its predecessor.<br><br><b>
  <i>"We were written for one another, and I wouldn't change one line in our romance novel. The good, the bad, the in between. It's ours. We own it."</i>
</b><br><br><i>*I was lucky to have had the opportunity to beta read for Gail McHugh*</i><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="9108001596150534282" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_513327523" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/513327523" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/513327523?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17267122-pulse">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer513327523" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6906846501144307790"><b>5 sexy and swoony stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/3a6764d0-6c5b-4e0f-9076-a2763a737c4b_zps6cc2dcc0.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406191i/792191.jpg' alt=' photo 3a6764d0-6c5b-4e0f-9076-a2763a737c4b_zps6cc2dcc0.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>After a killer cliffhanger, and waiting months and months for Pulse to be released, we finally get the conclusion to Gavin and Emily’s story. <br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>‘Do you know how scary it is to want something so bad you’re willing to change your whole life for it?’</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/>Emily met Gavin Blake in ‘Collide’. Emily was already in a relationship, and Gavin was not looking for a relationship, but for some unexplainable reason, they were drawn together. The feelings they had could not b</span>
  <span id="freeText6906846501144307790" style="display:none"><b>5 sexy and swoony stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/3a6764d0-6c5b-4e0f-9076-a2763a737c4b_zps6cc2dcc0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406191i/792191.jpg" alt=" photo 3a6764d0-6c5b-4e0f-9076-a2763a737c4b_zps6cc2dcc0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After a killer cliffhanger, and waiting months and months for Pulse to be released, we finally get the conclusion to Gavin and Emily’s story. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>‘Do you know how scary it is to want something so bad you’re willing to change your whole life for it?’</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Emily met Gavin Blake in ‘Collide’. Emily was already in a relationship, and Gavin was not looking for a relationship, but for some unexplainable reason, they were drawn together. The feelings they had could not be ignored, no matter how hard they tried. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/59376a22-6eba-4d5e-a08e-275ad061ed5c_zps602e4906.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406191i/792192.jpg" alt=" photo 59376a22-6eba-4d5e-a08e-275ad061ed5c_zps602e4906.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Due to some miscommunication and misunderstanding, things went a little crazy at the end of ‘Collide’. Now Gavin is gone. Emily is miserable. She can’t function without Gavin and no one is able to reach him. Emily does what she has to do. She goes to find her man. She gets to him, and they try to mend their relationship. Emily doesn’t want anyone but Gavin, not ever.<br><b>
  <blockquote>God, Gavin, I’m yours. Forever. No one else.</blockquote>
</b> Their reunion is quite memorable. <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Lovey%20for%20my%20books/Pulse-gif1_zps33678b08.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406191ra/792193.gif" alt=" photo Pulse-gif1_zps33678b08.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I’m going to fuck you right now, Emily. I’m going to bring you so much pleasure you’ll never think about walking away from me again.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>This book is HOT! Gavin Blake- DAMN. You are one sexy man! Sexy and sweet...<br><br>This is how I like to describe Mr. Blake...<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/52f3dc3d-65d7-46ad-8def-40b3d82f528b_zpsbeabfd23.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406191i/792194.jpg" alt=" photo 52f3dc3d-65d7-46ad-8def-40b3d82f528b_zpsbeabfd23.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>“I want to break the rules with you. Kiss you passionately every day. Make you smile when you’re about to cry. I want no regrets with us. I want us to laugh together until we can’t breathe and it hurts. No man will ever love you the way I’m going to love you.”</blockquote>
</i><br><br>I wanted everything to be perfect for these two- after all they had been through, I think they deserved it. But Emily learns something that will change her and Gavin’s life forever. Complications arise, things become challenging. <br><br>Gavin loves Emily in a way most women would only dream of. He is willing to stick by her side no matter what. In a situation where most men would have taken off, or at very least been hesitant to see how it went, Gavin was 100% committed. He made this book for me! The PERFECT man- period. He loves Emily with everything he has. He cherishes her. Protects her. Takes care of her. He’s still funny, cocky as hell, and too hot to handle, but he also shows more of his sweet and swoony side in this book. Ladies- you will not be disappointed with Mr. Blake.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/8578b395-b1b2-4a20-b721-583d2784df70_zpsb00a7a2a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406191i/792195.jpg" alt=" photo 8578b395-b1b2-4a20-b721-583d2784df70_zpsb00a7a2a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And Emily- book one she frustrated me to no end, this book, she didn’t. It was great to see her strength. She was much more likable and relatable. Olivia was still as funny and hilarious as ever, and Dillion was even MORE of an dickhead/douche bag, but I guess that was to be expected. In the end, I was very happy with how things turned out. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/172d4f1d-6a07-4630-ba8c-6fc960400179_zps5648c0b3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406191i/792196.jpg" alt=" photo 172d4f1d-6a07-4630-ba8c-6fc960400179_zps5648c0b3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I love Gail’s writing, it just has a flow to it, I just couldn’t put this one down. This story was much different than Collide, but I liked it just as much. Both are amazing 5 star reads for me. A beautiful tale of making the best out of a not ideal situation, trust, forgiveness, strength, and most importantly-unconditional love. Can’t wait to see whats next from this author! <br><br>And I can't forget to mention the bottle caps... I love the bottle caps! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/b77cb49b-9d28-45ff-978e-3a1afa063740_zpscca9afae.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406191i/792197.jpg" alt=" photo b77cb49b-9d28-45ff-978e-3a1afa063740_zpscca9afae.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2016-reads">2016-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=angst-overload">angst-overload</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=smexy-read">smexy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1654795866" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer401127019568112210"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"We were written for one another, and I wouldn't change one line in our romance novel. The good, the bad, the in between. It's ours. We own it."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>3 Stars</b><br/><br/>Warning: Potential spoilers ahead.<br/><br/>I'm a fan of the first book of this series (<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17158596.Collide__Collide___1_' title='Collide (Collide, #1) by Gail McHugh' rel='nofollow noopener'>Collide</a>). It was beautiful, with such emotional depth and enough angst. But I hate to say that the story kind of went downhill in this second and final installment. :(<br/><br/>First, let me cite the things that I loved about <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18775257.Pulse__Collide___2_' title='Pulse (Collide, #2) by Gail McHugh' rel='nofollow noopener'>Pulse</a>. I actually enjoyed the first half of</span>
  <span id="freeText401127019568112210" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"We were written for one another, and I wouldn't change one line in our romance novel. The good, the bad, the in between. It's ours. We own it."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>3 Stars</b><br><br>Warning: Potential spoilers ahead.<br><br>I'm a fan of the first book of this series (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17158596.Collide__Collide___1_" title="Collide (Collide, #1) by Gail McHugh" rel="nofollow noopener">Collide</a>). It was beautiful, with such emotional depth and enough angst. But I hate to say that the story kind of went downhill in this second and final installment. :(<br><br>First, let me cite the things that I loved about <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18775257.Pulse__Collide___2_" title="Pulse (Collide, #2) by Gail McHugh" rel="nofollow noopener">Pulse</a>. I actually enjoyed the first half of the book because the plot was exciting. In the beginning chapters we can see a different <b>Emily</b>-- one who pursues Gavin, desperately asking him for a second chance after what she did in the first book. I admit I really loved it when Gavin did not immediately succumb to her but instead made her emotionally suffer first before he took her back. That was what I was looking for. Make Emily suffer in order for her to realize what a spoiled, insensitive girl she was. *evil laughs. I also loved how strong Emily and Gavin became after the things they experienced and how they were able to handle Dillon.<br><br>But of course I developed negative feelings for this book especially because:<br><br>&gt; <b>There was too much cheesiness.</b> Don't get me wrong. I love cheese. But when it's overly done, nah. Give me a break! Most of the time Gavin and Emily kept reminding each other how much they love each other and it's already getting so annoying. Like, okay, I KNOW. Please.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417705430ra/12494335.gif" width="320" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>&gt; <b>The drama was overkill.</b> It went on and on and on... to the point where it already became frustrating.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465294677ra/19335523.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>&gt; <b>Too many unnecessary scenes.</b> Yep. Especially sex scenes. I've had enough already. Can we just move on?<br><br>... and when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[they discovered that Emily was pregnant and she didn't know who the father is...  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I was like<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465294831ra/19335565.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can say that Collide was a very good start but sad to say, the series' ending wasn't enough to give me the satisfaction. Yes, it has a good ending. Happy, even. But it didn't really captivate me. But despite my issues with this book, I still admire <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6860574.Gail_McHugh" title="Gail McHugh" rel="nofollow noopener">Gail McHugh</a> and her impeccable way of writing. She writes with emotions and she definitely nails an angst-ridden romance that will leave you breathless. <br><br><p>
  <a href="https://bibliopearl.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446199662i/16763926._SX540_.jpg" alt="Pearl's Book Journey (1)" width="380" height="190" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</p><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464648592i/19260109.png" width="250" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_665209500" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/665209500" />
    <a title="Anna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6744426-anna"><img alt="Anna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442117297p2/6744426.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/665209500?book_show_action=true">Jul 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anna" href="/user/show/6744426-anna">Anna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17267122-pulse">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer665209500" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9909164947054824322">This book picks up right where <b> COLLIDE</b> left off. I don't know about you but I had a serious case of the ickkkks after that double dip at the end of book 1. So I called for an immediate mental do-over. I was not satisfied!<br/><br/>I loved Gavin. He was perfect. But he was a little too perfect in this book.         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer661219083" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8584132853490074686">Well, I think Gail McHugh may have a mean streak hidden in there somewhere. There is an absolute gasp out loud Holy Fuck Moment in this book – I think Gail knew what our reaction to that would be and has had more than her fair share of secret giggles over that one!! Well, Gail – it definitely worked on me!! Colour me shocked!!<br/><br/>Right, back to the story – we rejoin Emily straight after she has walked out on Dillon. She goes straight to Gavin but the man is AWOL. He’s decided to disappear, leaving h</span>
  <span id="freeText8584132853490074686" style="display:none">Well, I think Gail McHugh may have a mean streak hidden in there somewhere. There is an absolute gasp out loud Holy Fuck Moment in this book – I think Gail knew what our reaction to that would be and has had more than her fair share of secret giggles over that one!! Well, Gail – it definitely worked on me!! Colour me shocked!!<br /><br />Right, back to the story – we rejoin Emily straight after she has walked out on Dillon. She goes straight to Gavin but the man is AWOL. He’s decided to disappear, leaving his cell phone on the tarmac, desperate to hide away from the crushing despair he is feeling. He believes Emily has gone ahead and married Douchenugget and just wants to lose himself in a haze of alcohol and easy women. Dillon shows up in Emily’s life again before she can find Gavin and shows us, once again, why he really is the spawn of the devil. Emily eventually manages to track Gavin down and runs to him in an attempt to reconcile and the story moves forward from here.<br /><br />I really loved this – Collide and Pulse together have made this one of the best series to be published this year. I enjoyed every second, completely lost myself in the story and got to know Emily, Gavin, Olivia and everyone else intimately, like they were my friends.<br /><br />It’s a beautiful story of emotional growth for Emily, a story of moving on, a story of stepping out of the darkness, blinking into the light – it’s uplifting and powerful and, most of all, a story of all-consuming love and passion and an absolute determination to be together despite all the odds. Emily pulls out all the stops to throw herself at Gavin’s mercy, to beg forgiveness and to atone for what has passed and I applauded her for it.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>Oh to be loved like a man like Gavin. I really do adore him! He’s still a Yankees-obsessed, bottle cap-giving wiseass but he’s so unbelievably charming and pantie- meltingly gorgeous. He’s all pure, primal, fierce and sexy alpha male and yet also incredibly tender, sensitive and caring. He wants nothing more than to soothe away all the hurt and make things right between him and Emily.</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />He cupped her cheeks, drawing her face closer to his. “I’m not sure you’ll ever understand, but I told you I need you more than I need my next breath. Since the day we met, from the second I laid eyes on you, there’s never been anyone else worth taking up a fucking inch of space in my mind.” He stroked his thumbs along her lips, laying his own against her forehead. “God created me to love you. Let me heal the cracks in your heart. I know this broken woman didn’t exist before Dillon. I refuse to believe that.”<br /><br />He’ll do just about anything for her and wants nothing more than a beautiful future with her believing firmly that what has gone before has only strengthened the bond that they now share.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>You told me once you thought you’d broken us. You didn’t break us, doll. You fixed us. Those bad minutes shaped us into what we are. They molded us into what we’re going to be together. We were written for one another, and I wouldn’t change one line in our romance novel. The good, the bad, the in between. It’s ours. We own it.</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />Le Sigh!! I just melted for how much Gavin single-mindedly adored Emily and knew that she was the one for him and would move just about heaven and earth to make things right between them. He’s so romantic, charismatic, charming. <br /><br />I loved this – couldn’t put it down. It’s emotional and tense and there’s always a nagging feeling that it could all just go horribly wrong at any second and I so wanted them to find that Happy Ever After that’s never seemed quite attainable for these two. For both of them, despite the pain and sorrow of the past, they were just so ready to find love with one another and it’s now perfect timing after all those missed first encounters and chances. <br /><br />Olivia is back, as colourful as ever with an incredible vocabulary of insulting names at the ready for Dillon – nothing he doesn’t deserve. My personal favourite were Dillmonster, Duckleberry Finn, Dick-wad and Dumbledick!<br /><br />4.5 awesome stars<br /><br />I just can’t wait to see what Gail does next!<br /><br /><i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a> or visit us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sinfullysexybookreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>.</i></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer640690025" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer18100875732436531239"><b>****4 Delectable Stars****</b><br/><br/><i>This Review is for both Collide and Pulse.</i><br/><br/><br/>I must admit I like the first book Collide much better than this second one. In the first installment of this duet there was still a mystery factor that kept me enticed throughout the story but by the time Pulse was starting all the masks had fallen and I discovered the true nature of each character. Overall this was a very enjoyable story were Gavin was my favorite protagonist and his delicious Caveman personality won me over.<br/><br/> </span>
  <span id="freeText18100875732436531239" style="display:none"><b>****4 Delectable Stars****</b><br><br><i>This Review is for both Collide and Pulse.</i><br><br><br>I must admit I like the first book Collide much better than this second one. In the first installment of this duet there was still a mystery factor that kept me enticed throughout the story but by the time Pulse was starting all the masks had fallen and I discovered the true nature of each character. Overall this was a very enjoyable story were Gavin was my favorite protagonist and his delicious Caveman personality won me over.<br><br> <a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/97960b7a-36b0-4061-82e7-69513c32e74e_zpssgiri91q.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435693286i/15371551.jpg" alt=" photo 97960b7a-36b0-4061-82e7-69513c32e74e_zpssgiri91q.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Gavin is a very successful businessman that after getting his heart broken has been all about working hard and playing harder. Lately he had been feeling like there was something missing from his life, so when he encounters the beautiful girl who is delivering his lunch he can't ignore the sparks flying the minute he set his eyes on her. Everything from her looks to her personality make him crazy with wanton, he can't control the need to make her his; the problem is she is already taken and by none other than one his best friends.<br><br>Emily had been dating Dillon for a while now and she's very much in love with him, so it's hard for her to understand the strong reaction she has every time Gavin is close to her. Gavin and Emily know that they shouldn't feel anything for each other so they settle for a friendship that with time will turn dangerous and hard to resist the carnal feelings it evokes in them. What happens when her boyfriend Dillon's mask starts to come off and Emily and everyone else around them notice he's not the good and honest man everyone thinks he is?<br><br>This story starts as a little bit of a love triangle, but then only true love will be the one to conquer. What will happen when Emily is finally able to be with the one man she truly loves, will it be easy for her to fight and win for the truth burning inside her heart? <br><br>As far as the story goes, it was very well written in my opinion. The characters were all well developed but that doesn't mean I was a fan of them all. Emily, I wish she could been stronger at times but I understood the role her past had played into her actions. Dillon, I absolutely hated; he will probably win first place on most annoying characters , ever. And Gavin, well, he takes the crown as most delectable Alpha Male. I really enjoyed this story and for sure I will recommended it to all my friends. </span>
  <a data-text-id="18100875732436531239" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer18293311298422684240">Collide gave us a new book boyfriend, the swoon some and deliciously HOT Gavin ♥ It also gave us the cliff hanger from hell!!! I was desperate to get my hands on the sequel!! After much anticipation I was so happy to reconnect with Emily and Gavin and live out their happy ever after. (Well I hoped they would get a hea!)<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409598i/802064._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I love the theme of fate running through this story, the idea that there is someone for everyone, you just have to wait for your paths to cross at the right moment and if you miss</span>
  <span id="freeText18293311298422684240" style="display:none">Collide gave us a new book boyfriend, the swoon some and deliciously HOT Gavin ♥ It also gave us the cliff hanger from hell!!! I was desperate to get my hands on the sequel!! After much anticipation I was so happy to reconnect with Emily and Gavin and live out their happy ever after. (Well I hoped they would get a hea!)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409598i/802064._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love the theme of fate running through this story, the idea that there is someone for everyone, you just have to wait for your paths to cross at the right moment and if you miss your moment, there will always be another chance. <br><br><i>I LOVE that and believe in it!!! Yes, I'm a romantic at heart ♥</i><br><br>The other major theme is domestic violence....<br><i>"Did you know one in three women wind up in a mentally or physically abusive relationship?" ~ Emily</i><br>This was dealt with extremely sensitively and in a subtle way throughout the story, adding to the emotion of it all.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Gavin Blake .....You're gentle. You're kind. You're strong and witty. You're personable and warm. You can reduce most females into blithering puddles of goo with the simplest words."</i>
</b><br><br>Gavin is adorable and gorgeous and so very, very sweet. ♥<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409598i/802066._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Are you swooning???</i> <br><br>He also has very gifted fingers and,<i> "...a very talented tongue."</i> Oh yes!!! Ladies, he knows how to please which makes for a smoking HOT read!! Fabulous!!<br><br>Gavin and Emily have a HUGE amount of LOVE for each other....it oozes off the pages beautifully and the writing and sentiment is really quite stunning and profound in places.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Our past is imperfect, but our future's breathtaking." ~ Emily</i>
</b> Beautiful words ♥<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409598i/802067._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>For me personally, I would have liked a little more angst and some more conflict to make the reunion so much sweeter. It was all moving along so nicely (maybe too nicely?) I was waiting for an aghhhh moment....I felt like something drastic was going to happen....there was a WTF moment that made me cry (I can't say anymore about that without spoiling the story) but....well everything else was just lovely and wonderful......I loved the whole drama with <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the baby and, whose the Daddy?....But, really, it had to belong to Gavin or I think there would have been a riot!! lol <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br>♥ All in all I would say if you loved Collide then you have to read this because Gavin is simply divine and the love between the characters is immensely beautiful. <br><br><i>If you haven't read Collide....what are you waiting for it's AMAZING!!!!!!</i><br><br><br><b>
  <i>Bottle Tops</i>
</b> and <b>
  <i>Twenty Questions</i>
</b> create some very memorable, sweet moments....if you've read Collide and Pulse then I need say no more.....ahhhh.....sweet memories *Sigh*<br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409598i/802069._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>

<span id="freeTextContainer3541504351910105538">Okay, give me a moment to breathe.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428713ra/858084.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This was so, SOOO, good. I’m not completely recovered yet, so I’ll probably have some trouble doing this review. Mainly, because I have no idea what to say except: <i>awesome</i>.<br/>The book started right after the end of the first, when Emily finally got some sense in his head and left Dillon and gone to fight for Gavin. <br/>She knows that she was stupid and did a lot of things wrong, she knows that Gavin probably won’t take her back, especially when she did a lot mistakes. </span>
  <span id="freeText3541504351910105538" style="display:none">Okay, give me a moment to breathe.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428713ra/858084.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was so, SOOO, good. I’m not completely recovered yet, so I’ll probably have some trouble doing this review. Mainly, because I have no idea what to say except: <i>awesome</i>.<br>The book started right after the end of the first, when Emily finally got some sense in his head and left Dillon and gone to fight for Gavin. <br>She knows that she was stupid and did a lot of things wrong, she knows that Gavin probably won’t take her back, especially when she did a lot mistakes. But damn, if she isn’t going to try.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428713i/858085.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But Dillon’s ghost is still very present and when <i>something</i> happens they’ll will have to fight harder than ever (which isn’t easy) for their relationship. <br>And this “little thing” has the power of getting them together… or make them falling apart for good. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428713i/858086.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved this book even more than the first one. I didn't know that would be possible considering that the first one was real great. <br>It wasn't as much angsty (thank god!), but it was way sweeter and romantic. And the steam was better. Believe there was a lot of “shmexy” scenes. <br><br>Emily really redeemed herself in my eyes and she had a great attitude through this whole book<br>Gavin, well… was even more perfect than before. <i>*le sigh*</i><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428713ra/858087.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The supportive characters were great in this book as well, probably more than in the first even. Did I already told that I love Olivia? For some seconds she really pissed me off, but other than that she was as great as before. <br>Dillon was the exactly same asshole he was in the first one. Probably even more. Luckily he doesn’t appear as much as in the first. But all the times he appears were that number of times too many. Stupid asshole. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428713ra/858088.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, I can only say that this was an amazing ending for a perfect series. I loved the conclusion, loved how the characters ending, loved everything. <br>I was great to get to know Molly’s and Mrs. Tall, Dark and Fuckable Handsome’s story. I’ll re-read them a lot of times, for sure. :)</span>

<div id="review_666764767" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/666764767?book_show_action=true">Jul 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela Richardson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela Richardson" href="/user/show/14805495-angela-richardson">Angela Richardson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17267122-pulse">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer666764767" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5168412558925970633">3.5 stars. *SPOILERS - READ AT OWN RISK* <br/>After some reflection have bumped up an extra half star purely for GAVIN.<br/><br/>Firstly I want to say my rating is not based on the writing. I LOVE Gail McHugh's writing style and way with words. Its beautiful. Its sexy as hell, and her storytelling skills are superb! Really amazing!<br/>I will read anything she writes.<br/><br/>The reason I gave this one three stars is because I'm the type of girl who doesn't need the fairy tale ending. I don't need a sequel to be wrapped up </span>
  <span id="freeText5168412558925970633" style="display:none">3.5 stars. *SPOILERS - READ AT OWN RISK* <br>After some reflection have bumped up an extra half star purely for GAVIN.<br><br>Firstly I want to say my rating is not based on the writing. I LOVE Gail McHugh's writing style and way with words. Its beautiful. Its sexy as hell, and her storytelling skills are superb! Really amazing!<br>I will read anything she writes.<br><br>The reason I gave this one three stars is because I'm the type of girl who doesn't need the fairy tale ending. I don't need a sequel to be wrapped up in a perfect package to get closure and feel complete and all warm and fuzzy. I don't need to be told on every page how much the two main characters love each other, are meant for each other, and are sexually in sync with each other. I don't need a whole story to convince me of that. And there is nothing wrong with story filled with LOTS of love, great sex and a big HEA. But I guess I was just hoping for a sequel a bit different from the normal kind of sequel. <br>I also felt like the drama was pretty minor. I already knew by the end of book 1. that there was going to be a bun in her oven, and I knew it would end up being Gavin's. So when Dillon tried to interfere, I knew it would go no where....<br> <br>I will admit, I thought the story got REALLY ballsy at 80%!!!!! yeah - I'm going to say it - I was disappointed when it didn't happen (I'll duck now so you can throw knives at me)!!! Cause my first thought was - OH NO MS MCHUGH - YOU DIDNT JUST DO THAT!! (excited &amp; unexpected happy dance for the massive left hand turn) - and then it was - oh - she really didn't do that... well.....ohhhh....k. and - we're back on track. And that pissed me off, and not in a good way. <br><br>But my initial thoughts after I read it were:- <br>1.The counting drove me *INSANE*. <br>2. It's a bit too sugary and predictable for my personal taste (but that's just me so do not let that deter you from reading it) <br>and 3. I felt like there was heaps more filler in this story than the first. <br><br>But GAVIN really carried this book. He was beyond the perfect kind of Alpha male. I really loved him!!<br><br>So if you love sequels which feel like they will 'complete you' and give you all the closure you need - then PULSE will be perfect for you. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/2u7Smei" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429054ra/859123.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I would recommend it! Especially for swoon worthy Gavin (sigh...)<br>3.5 stars :-)</span>
  <a data-text-id="5168412558925970633" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1271231314" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1271231314" />
    <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu"><img alt="Ramona Popescu " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594649997p2/33526516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1271231314?book_show_action=true">May 03, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ramona Popescu " href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu">Ramona Popescu </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=man-crush">man-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=love-this-series">love-this-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=hot-romance">hot-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1271231314" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11589653401937422002">One of my favorite book has a sequel and I am so excited to share with you my opinion about it.<br/>Collide was awesome in all the right places and I fell in love with Gavin and Emily almost immediately, because as a couple they are intense and sweet.<br/><br/>The last chapter from Collide managed to cut my blood circulation and I was hungry to read Pulse.. I was so sorry with what happened to Gavin and really mad at Emily for making this happen. Now, we embark in a very adventurous attempt to get Gavin back, </span>
  <span id="freeText11589653401937422002" style="display:none">One of my favorite book has a sequel and I am so excited to share with you my opinion about it.<br>Collide was awesome in all the right places and I fell in love with Gavin and Emily almost immediately, because as a couple they are intense and sweet.<br><br>The last chapter from Collide managed to cut my blood circulation and I was hungry to read Pulse.. I was so sorry with what happened to Gavin and really mad at Emily for making this happen. Now, we embark in a very adventurous attempt to get Gavin back, and I am all aboard with it. <br><br>Emily needs Gavin forgiveness and heads out to find him. You have to read the book to find out what happens next, but it is worth every page. At the beginning, he find a wrecked Gavin, that lost all hope in being with the woman he loves. He is not very confident in their love, and very afraid that Emily will leave him again. A second attempt may destroy him completely. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1476443313i/20842176.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>From my point of view he forgave her too easily.. I mean.. She dumped him without accepting a justification, without talking to him, rushed the marriage plans she has with her boyfriend and just shut him out. I was extremely sad to witness Gavin's hurt and just so mad at Emily.. She should have been more mature and not fall victim to anger and hurt. But leaving this aside, I thought that Emily will grow on me again, and just be patience to see how the action develops. <br><br>Gavin, if possible, is even more amazing than in Collide and made me fall in love with him even more. He deserves 90% of the rating that I gave to this book, because he is perfect. He doesn't want want to be away from Emily anymore and will do anything to keep her, to protect her from the ones that want to harm her. He is so confident and determined to show her the bright future they have ahead, and he is just perfect. Half through the book, we are faced with a twist that felt us OMG, and in this situation we she what a great and lovable man he is. <br><br>He is willing to except anything from Emily, if it means being with her forever. There is something you don't find every day and spoke to highly about him. I hope he exists in real life and that some girl gets to enjoy him:) <br>I found a more mature Emily, a more determined and confident one, that managed to keep her fears aside and confront her problems. She made a great team with Gavin and I was happy that all the fears were gone between them.<br><br>I enjoyed how the plot developed, the twist that blow my mind away and made a very good subject to focus on. The mystery behind it was a stroke of genius for Gail's part and added to the drama of the series. <br><br>Everything was perfect beside that one chapter that took like 5 year of my life in just 10 minutes, and after reaching the next one, 5 years more to adjust to reality. I mean, it was that necessary? Never mind.. I love this book with everything in it and totally recommend it for the awesome hero, great plot and extremely intense love scenes.. augggh..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479123324i/21149668._SX540_.png" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>For more reviews please check <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com">https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="11589653401937422002" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
