<div id="review_665326468" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/665326468" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/665326468?book_show_action=true">Jul 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17267122-pulse">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer665326468" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16910279039968804667">5 AWESOME STARS FOR STORYLINE.<br/>3 STARS FOR LITERARY ANNOYANCES.<br/><br/>Can I just start out by saying Gavin is perfection, ladies? This man delivers it all.....hot sexy tattooed body hidden by his Armani suit, successful, sweet, a touch arrogant, humorous, and loyal to the end.....swoon. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&current=tumblr_mjyqpaDbm51qb6vvvo2_250-Coacutepia_zps49c967e4.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/638825.gif' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>My Gavin-<br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&current=555850954e2ce3fabbc3440721ded95a_zpscca62f7d.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428850i/858411._SX540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Pulse starts off on the heels of the cliffy we all endured in Collide. Don't read further if you've not read Collide as it has some spoilers. Dillon was a total douche and Emily has walked out on him the</span>
  <span id="freeText16910279039968804667" style="display:none">5 AWESOME STARS FOR STORYLINE.<br>3 STARS FOR LITERARY ANNOYANCES.<br><br>Can I just start out by saying Gavin is perfection, ladies? This man delivers it all.....hot sexy tattooed body hidden by his Armani suit, successful, sweet, a touch arrogant, humorous, and loyal to the end.....swoon. <br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_mjyqpaDbm51qb6vvvo2_250-Coacutepia_zps49c967e4.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/638825.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>My Gavin-<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=555850954e2ce3fabbc3440721ded95a_zpscca62f7d.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428850i/858411._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Pulse starts off on the heels of the cliffy we all endured in Collide. Don't read further if you've not read Collide as it has some spoilers. Dillon was a total douche and Emily has walked out on him the eve of their wedding. Emily can't marry that man. He's a monster. What a huge mistake. Is it too late to get Gavin back? Can she find him since he walked out at the rehearsal dinner? Will he slam the door in her face? She's sure going to try.....<br><br>My Dillon-<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=823569617df54974423ae3d6693f972b_zps939634c6.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428850i/858412._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>My Emily-<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=b863c8024bd95aa91f3729112b706220_zps7566046f.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428850i/858413._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Huge things happen throughout this book and no spoilers here. It's vague but their story has to be experienced as it comes. Even if some of those events made me want to throw my kindle against the hardest wall I could find. <br><b><br>What I loved about this book-</b><br><br>-The love story. I loved the progression of everything. It was well paced, the sex scenes very erotic and captivating. The character development of Emily, Gavin and Dillon was all stellar. I mean, Gavin surely stole the show but how can he not?<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=d88e5250dbb52fbb52b5769580bd0434_zps6cab412b.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428850i/858414._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I loved the cutesie little "inside jokes and games" between Emily and Gavin. It was realistic and endearing.<br>My highlights.....<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=2536cde222ed531ed6bc0dc8249a6937_zps39ed2ed8.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428850i/858415.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=f928682b1e0b4a93837dcfdb6e880e16_zps1b13fca3.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428850i/858416.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=2a8ed6d22baae7bcfb6863490a6a29af_zps7da6f52d.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428850i/858417.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>-The ending was PERFECTION. Loved loved loved it. <br><br>Now to be the buzz kill....<br><br><b>What I detested about this book-</b><br><br>-The annoying overuse of similes. I mean EVERYTHING was "blank like a blank...." It just reminded me of my high schooler's English papers. Trying to add that but it just was overused and strange. I highlighted a few as an example...<br><br><i>"Gavin's mouth coated her's like a glaze of honey."<br>"His heat surrounded her like a heavy down comforter."<br>"Her words zipped from her mouth faster than a shot of lightning"</i><br><br>I mean, like multiple similes in one page. It was just excessive and distracting. <br><br>-Second, there was a fair share of typos and grammatical errors. To the point it annoyed me. I can skim past a couple but beyond that, get a BFF beta reader prior to publication!<br><br>-Third, and what made me go batshit cray-cray was the scene towards the end. Do not hit the spoiler unless you've read the book! Or maybe you should as it may save you the anguish and anger I felt with this author. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ That entire fricking chapter devoted to Gavin's motorcycle accident, ensuing hospitalization and tragic death? Seriously? I mean if you want to throw in drama, fine, make something like that a quickie paragraph or two but to devote basically a chapter to a FAKE EVENT, A NIGHTMARE? That was just MEAN and UNNECESSARY. That made me so mad, I almost chucked the book and asked Amazon for a refund. SO <b>NOT </b>COOL! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_inline_mmt75uHa0L1qz4rgp_zps893792ef.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428850ra/858418.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Third, although this book had a bit less of the overuse of drama and angst, it still used EVERY twist we see in other storylines to add angst. It got old. I saw EVERYTHING coming. Shoot, the main plot twist (ya know, the "little tidbit" I'm referring to if you read this book) I saw coming in the first book. It was just way too predictable. <br><br>Fourth, and I hope it's not too picky but the use of Massive Attack's "Angel" as a song he listens to while thinking of her....Um, that's been used in two other romance novels in the past couple years. Find something new...not another author's song choice. Good song, just not original. <br><br>Yes, it sounds as if my negatives outweigh my positives but they really don't. Did they annoy me? Yes. They just hugely prevented this book from being one of my favorites of this year. And sadly, easily prevented on a literary standpoint. The story was SPECTACULAR. I shall miss Gavin.....<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=b4e80c1e91d059a5dfff21164490f4e6_zps8a820447.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428850i/858419._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16910279039968804667" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

I truly loved how Gavin picked Em up and never let her forget how much he loves her. He did it not only in word but action. Truly, one of the best book romances ever. They were both phenomenal and so different.<br/><br/>Whilst <i>Collide</i> was angsty and frustrating, <i>Pulse</i> was heart warming, full of hope, despite the heartache, deliciously sexy and just a total page turner.<br/><br/><i>Pulse</i> picks up right where <i>Collide</i> ended. We begin w</span>
  <span id="freeText9437575533787813937" style="display:none"><span>[image error]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425972i/850556._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425972i/850557._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>WARNING: CONTAINS SPOILERS FOR BOOK #1!!!</b><br><br>Read Collide (Collide #1) review here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/2013/07/24/collide-collide-1-by-gail-mchugh-%E2%9C%B0%E2%9C%B0%E2%9C%B0%E2%9C%B0%E2%9C%B0/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com...</a><br><br>Soooooooo good!!!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425972i/850558.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Honestly, this series had be completely hooked! I really don't know if I preferred book #1 or book #2. They were both phenomenal and so different.<br><br>Whilst <i>Collide</i> was angsty and frustrating, <i>Pulse</i> was heart warming, full of hope, despite the heartache, deliciously sexy and just a total page turner.<br><br><i>Pulse</i> picks up right where <i>Collide</i> ended. We begin with Emily as she follows through on her decision to leave Douchebag Dillon, in pursuit of our lovely Gavin. And we're off. And whilst Gavin continues to be amazeballs, Dillon continues to be a complete prick!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I loved you, and you became everything you said you never would!"</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425972i/850559.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Gavin and Emily's reunion wasn't a wham-bam-thank-you-m'am. But it didn't drag out. Thank God. I was worried that the whole of Pulse was going to be Gavin twoing and froing about whether he wanted Emily back. Of course, bridges had been burnt and trust had been broken, so it wasn't all smooth sailing, but it wasn't without it's heartache.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"After I'm finished fucking you, I'm going to make love to you. From the minute my body touched yours, there was never going to be anyone else. I'm in love with you, but I have to fuck you first. Do you understand me?"</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>At about the 30% mark I was loving it, but thinking, okay, this is good, but I kind of feel like we've come to a conclusion right now... how wrong was I?! Jeez, poor Gavin and Emily really can't catch a break!<br><br>I was totally blindsided by the plot for this book. Shit a brick! I really didn't see it coming. I don't know why, looking back, now I know, I can totally see the clues... but anyway, I didn't guess and I was shocked. <br><br>I felt so sorry for Emily. She hadn't done anything wrong and yet she finds herself in an absolutely devastating situation. But, hey, I'm not in love with Emily, so whilst I felt for her, my heart just shattered for Gavin. Ohhh, my poor poor baby. :(<br><br>I <i>loved</i> the solidarity between Gavin and Emily in this book. They talked, they communicated, they dealt with situations as best they could, like rational adults, despite the shitty hand they were dealt. It was so refreshing! There was no ridiculous over reactions, no miscommunications, no petty issues... the problems they faced were real, heartbreaking and the whole things just made me want to fangirl all over Gail McHugh!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"We were written for one another, and I wouldn't change one line in our romance novel. The good, the bad, the in between. It's ours. We own it."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I <i>think</i> I might have mentioned, that I love Gavin... but just incase you didn't get that memo. I fucking <i>
  <b>love</b>
</i> Gavin Blake! Okay? He's perfect. Like, in such a way that he has flaws, is over protective, flies off the handle sometimes, totally stole his best friend's girlfriend, but is <i>still</i> just perfect. And let's not pretend we're not impressed by the size of his... bank account! (Get your mind out of the gutter, ladies!) It makes me sad that we can't conjure him up, using our imagination, into a living, breathing, real-life human being! These book boyfriends could really begin to depress a girl if we're not careful.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I want to break the rules with you. Kiss you passionately every day. Make you smile when you're about to cry. I want no regrets with us. I want us to laugh together until we can't breathe and it hurts. No man will ever love you the way I'm going to love you, Emily. You're it. My last. My forever."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425972i/850560._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Emily is so very broken in this book. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425972i/850561.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She's suffered a helluva ordeal and it's taken it's toll. And seeing Gavin build her back up, restore her self worth, convey his adoration for her, is just breath taking. He's so determined that she won't come to any more harm. *swoon* I love it. I know, that's all I keep saying. I love it. I love it. I love it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I'm so sorry. I'm sorry that out of any girl in this world you couldn't fallen in love with, you chose me."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>There was one scene in this book that made me cry happy tears like a little bitch!! Oh, the sweetness was just off the freakin' scale. It was two o'clock in the morning, I was blubbing like an idiot and Mr. Smitten rolled over, looked at me like I had three heads, rolled his eyes, said 'Can you cry a bit quieter please?' and went back to sleep. I continued to sob through my big stupid grin! I cry at books quite a lot when they're sad, but I can't recall many books that have made me cry happy tears. It's just that damn beautiful to see Emily and Gavin find some happiness after all of the ugly they endured.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I didn't think it was possible, but I'm more in love with you now than before. You've rocked my entire world, Emily Cooper."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425972i/850562._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And lastly, but absolutely definitely not least, holy hotness!!! There are some sexy as hell scenes in this book. The car scene! Oh my Christ!!! Phew.<br><br>Oh, wait, I know I said 'lastly', but, just quickly... The epilogue is entitled <i>
  <b>Molly and Mr. Tall, Dark and Fuckable Handsome's Epilogue</b>
</i>! I love that! :D<br><br>Right, do you think I should probably stop typing now? I mean, if that review hasn't sold it to, I'm think you're pretty un-impress-able! I could go on... but I don't think it's necessary. There's a lot of heartache, and <i>Collide</i> is maddening beyond belief at times. You <i>will</i> want to push Emily in front of a bus at various intervals and Dillon just needs castrating from the beginning... but it's so totally worth it. Pinky promise!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425972i/850563._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>Pulse</i> Statistics</b><br><b>Steam Rating (out of 5):</b> ♥♥♥♥♥<br><b>Ending:</b> HEA<br><b>Series:</b> ✓ (<i>Collide</i> series)<br><b>Reading Order:</b><br>Book #1 - <i>Collide</i><br>Book #2 - <i>Pulse</i><br><b>Can this be read as a standalone?</b> No<br><b>Themes:</b><br>Love triangle<br>Controlling partner<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Pregnancy <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Warning. This book includes... </b><br>Domestic violence<br>Sexual content<br><b>Writing:</b> Great<br><br><b>Blog Tour Giveaway</b><br>As part of the <i>Pulse</i> blog tour, Gail McHugh is giving away a $200 visa gift card, a $100 Amazon or Barns and Noble Giftcard, a Kindle Fire and a signed set of Pulse and Collide signed paperbacks.<br>Don't forget to enter here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.rafflecopter.com/rafl/share-code/MWVlYWZkNzhmMGIyOGNjYjNlMDU3YWEwYmUwNmZmOjM5/">http://www.rafflecopter.com/rafl/shar...</a><br><br><b>Teaser Alert</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>With an equally devious brow lifted, Gavin ran a hand through his messy hair, and leaned back against<br><br>the headboard, the grin on his mouth wide. “These gifts wouldn’t happen to include a black laced <br><br>ensemble worn by you, double ‘A’ batteries and your ‘shmexy’ legs shaking uncontrollably around my <br><br>head, would they?”<br><br>Eyes wide, Emily belted out a laugh. All humor left her face as she <br><br>slowly crawled onto the bed. With the bag in one hand, she took the other and slightly lowered his <br><br>sweatpants. He buried his hands in her hair <br><br>as she hovered, lightly skimming her tongue along the edge of the evil looking beast’s wings. In all its <br><br>evilness, it tasted like the sweetest cotton candy in her mouth. <br><br>Emily brought her eyes up to his, their light, blue sexual intensity shocking through her system. She <br><br>smiled. “So you never told me why you got this particular tattoo on your body.”<br><br>Gavin blinked, a rush of puffed air escaping his mouth. “Are you honestly going to ask me that after <br><br>you just achingly licked your way up my body?”<br><br> “What?” Emily giggled, straddling his waist. Are you saying I’m not the first to lick it?”<br><br>In one quick movement, Gavin slipped his arm behind her waist, flipping her onto her back. <br><br>Emily gasped, her heart nearly stopping as he hovered above her, lightly brushing his mouth against <br><br>hers. “Oh my God,” she breathed. “I was right. You are crazy.”<br><br>“And you’re trying to kill me with your questions,” Gavin countered, now nipping at her bottom lip, <br><br>which she started to realize was something he loved to do. “You’re no longer allowed to say the <br><br>words ‘lick it’ while in my presence. Is this understood, Miss Cooper?”<br><br>His demand drifted over her like a caress, however, she was about to push a few buttons. She popped a <br><br>brow, her mouth curled into a smirk. “Lick… it… Caveman.”</i>

</a><br><br><br>He is PERFECT, ABSOLUTELY PERFECT. He is a man that is so in love, that he will do whatever is necessary to stand by the woman who he loves, Emily. He has enough conviction, love, passion, desire, heart, and sexiness to make you swoon for days, yes, days!!<br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Ladies/Nina-Dobrev-nina-dobrev-8213695-1024-768_zps3d1a7ab5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Emily has done a lot of growing up in this book. She spends a lot of time apologizing for not listening to her mind and heart about her prior relationship, the one that almost robbed her of her future happiness with Gavin. <br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/6e958b9b-97e6-48a6-93ba-1fb3f20a91f4_zpsa29193ca.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>They do get back together relatively quickly but I loved it because the relationship between Emily and Gavin is a beautiful read. Gail McHugh writes from the heart and makes the love between Gavin and Emily come alive. There were so many passages that made me cringe, cry, swoon, melt and truly experience their passion. Thank you Gail for making this a phenomenal series in my eyes, even with the WTF scene that I forgive you for. <br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/image_zps96a3f879.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/image_zpsbd7b8045.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I loved -<br>Twenty Questions<br>Count downs<br>Bottle Caps<br>"Sweets"<br>Green Minivan<br>"Shmexy"<br>Caveman<br><br><b>"You told me once you thought you'd broken us. You didn't break us doll. You fixed us. Those bad minutes shaped us into what we are. They molded us into what we're going to be together. We were written for one another, and I wouldn't change one line in our romance novel. The good, the bad, and the in between. It's our. We own it."</b><br><br>There were so many memorable passages that I could quote for days so my recommendation would be to read this series asap!! Gavin Blake is one Hot, Shmexy, Walking Wiseass, King of Swoon!!!<br><br><br>BR with my "Shmexy" ladies Barb, Jxxx and Anna♥<br><br></span>

<div id="review_521483786" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13629682-ang-sizzling-pages"><img alt="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1541857150p2/13629682.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/521483786?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ang (Sizzling Pages)" href="/user/show/13629682-ang-sizzling-pages">Ang (Sizzling Pages)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17267122-pulse">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer521483786" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16527451903902292136">For more reviews please visit and join<br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://angelas-sizzling-pages.blogspot.com'>http://angelas-sizzling-pages.blogspo...</a><br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.sizzlingpages.com'>http://www.sizzlingpages.com</a><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383074519i/6374934._SX540_.png' width='200' height='150' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/>5 out of 5 Pulsating Stars<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382936086i/6290151.png' width='175' height='100' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/>Oh sweet Gavin, I adore you and your bottle caps. <br/><br/>Gavin is a sexy, intelligent, powerful, cocky, yet gentle soul. Each time he calls Emily “doll” or "sweets", I swoon. What I admired most about Gavin was how he stood firm by Emily's side, even after she totally shattered his heart. All his sugary sweetness gave me a toothache. I craved for him to possess a more al</span>
  <span id="freeText16527451903902292136" style="display:none">For more reviews please visit and join<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://angelas-sizzling-pages.blogspot.com">http://angelas-sizzling-pages.blogspo...</a><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.sizzlingpages.com">http://www.sizzlingpages.com</a><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383074519i/6374934._SX540_.png" width="200" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>5 out of 5 Pulsating Stars<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382936086i/6290151.png" width="175" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Oh sweet Gavin, I adore you and your bottle caps. <br><br>Gavin is a sexy, intelligent, powerful, cocky, yet gentle soul. Each time he calls Emily “doll” or "sweets", I swoon. What I admired most about Gavin was how he stood firm by Emily's side, even after she totally shattered his heart. All his sugary sweetness gave me a toothache. I craved for him to possess a more alpha personality, but loved him regardless. Gavin Blake is the epitome of the perfect book boyfriend.<br> <br>At the end of “Collide”, I was ranting and screaming…Emily, get your head out of your ass! Dillon…you are a huge Dumbledick son-of-a-bitch. Ugh, what a frustrating ending and I could not wait to read the continuing love story between Gavin Blake and Emily Cooper. <br><br>The story line in "Pulse" took an unexpected turn for me. I did not envision the way the story played out at all. I was pleased none-the-less (Except for Dillon - I want revenge…grrr! I wanted to see him hang from the highest rafter). <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383074565i/6374949.jpg" width="300" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Emily’s character surprised me. After all the experiences she had endured by the hands of Dillon, she grew to be strong-willed and did not crumble. Her strength comes from within, but also from Gavin. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383074565i/6374950.jpg" width="300" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Gavin's persona amazed me as well. His love for Em changed him, from a playboy to a dedicated boyfriend. I was in awe of his determination to move their relationship forward, despite all the trials and tribulations they suffered. He was unwavering regardless of Dillon’s efforts. It is his undying love for Emily that gave Gavin the fortitude to put back the pieces of her broken spirit.<br> <br>As fate steps in and plays a role in turning Emily's life upside down, it is Gavin that holds the key to her happiness and hope. Gavin's forgiveness is a blessing to Emily.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383074565i/6374951.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“You make me feel like I’m in a dream,...Like I’m sleepwalking and I don’t even know it.” “I’m able to close my eyes and just… trust you. You’re the color on my blank canvas, the light in my dark, the air in my lungs, and I almost let you go. I almost erased us from ever happening. I can’t imagine not having you here with me. Please tell me you know how much I love you, Gavin. I need to hear it right now. Please.”</i><br><br>Gavin is a sexy, hopeless romantic. He has such a sensual way with words that are panty melting. His proclamations of love, as well as his actions, touched my soul.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383074565i/6374952._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“Emily Cooper, the only thing you have to fear is how much I’m going to love you for the rest of your life. And… how many times I’m going to make those legs shake."<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383074565i/6374953._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>“Look at me, Emily... Right there, doll. You said every look I’ve given you was without judgment. Well, every look you’ve given me is untouched, pure in all it is for my eyes. You look at me like you’ve never seen a man before. There’s no way for me, as a man, to ever explain what that feels like.” He reached for her hand and laid it against his heart. “You said every touch I’ve given was without judgment. Every time you touch me, your hands shake. You have no idea how that makes me shake. I’m not talking sexually, either. You shake everything I’ve ever know myself to be.”</i><br><br> O.M.G....Sigh.... Gavin - how can I not love you? <br><br>This story had it all..... Angst, steamy love scenes, immense sorrow, boundless joy, nail biting moments and a happily ever after that swelled my heart. I could not put this book down and I long to see what Gail McHugh has in store for us next.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383074565i/6374954.png" width="100" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="16527451903902292136" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9ikapSB9ybMRGW5qLOTWIQX6ULdTG0hL0sWkbTsdgLkHLEYsu3GQzGAHAfKeQUWW9ltENYHLLpT0c0wZsePc+w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('TyEaWKnXnSBKexh6209EBwIznBySVr2GFYC1zzgNpCO+JEbRMtvEXztld+Jp6tew8ZKInkCG21kzNl27svP4YQ==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText2740627411653859292" style="display:none">A self-proclaimed chocoholic, married mother of three, and a lover of writing for as far back as she can remember, Gail McHugh is the author of two New York Times bestselling novels. The COLLIDE series (which includes COLLIDE and PULSE), was acquired by Atria Books on September 17th, 2013.<br /><br />“The first of two sexy contemporary romances about a woman torn between her seemingly perfect boyfriend and a dark, mysterious stranger who will stop at nothing to have her.” - Publishers Weekly on COLLIDE, a Top 10 Romance pick! <br /><br />Gail's next novel (also publishing through Atria Books), AMBER TO ASHES, is slated to release June 9th, 2015.<br /><br />You can follow Gail on the below social media sites and email: <br />Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/AuthorGailMcHugh?ref=hl">https://www.facebook.com/AuthorGailMc...</a><br />Twitter: @Gail_McHugh<br />Amazon: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amazon.com/author/gailmchugh">amazon.com/author/gailmchugh</a><br />Email: author.gail.mchugh@gmail.com <br />And her blog at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.authorgailmchugh.com">www.authorgailmchugh.com</a><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
